<script type="text/javascript">

    var jqueryFunction;
    var timer;

    $().ready(function () {
        //jQuery function
        jqueryFunction = function (_msg) {

            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(function () { $('#psearch').load('http://www.fangraphs.com/quickplayersearch.aspx?name=' + encodeURIComponent(_msg)); }, 250);

        }

    })

    $(window).load(function () {
        $('#menublog').load('http://www.fangraphs.com/headerlive.aspx?type=3');

        $('#menuteams').empty();
        $('#menuteams').load('http://www.fangraphs.com/headerlive.aspx?type=1');

        $('#menugames').empty();
        $('#menugames').load('http://www.fangraphs.com/headerlive.aspx?type=2');

        $('#psearch').load('http://www.fangraphs.com/headerlive.aspx?type=4');
    });

    function KeyIt(e) {

        var evt;
        var evc;

        if (window.event) {
            evt = window.event; // IE
            evc = window.event.keyCode;
        }
        else {
            evt = e;   // Firefox
            evc = e.which;
        }

        if (evc == 13) {
            evt.returnValue = false;
            evt.cancel = true;
            SearchIt();
        }
        else {
            SearchItBar();
        }

    }

    function SearchIt() {

        top.location.href = 'http://www.fangraphs.com/players.aspx?lastname=' + document.getElementById('psbox').value;

    }

    function SearchItBar() {

        jqueryFunction(document.getElementById('psbox').value);

    }


</script>

    function setAverage(t) {
        var elements;
        var browserCheck = (document.all) ? 1 : 0;
        if (t == '*') {
            elements = (ie) ? document.all : document.getElementsByTagName('*');
        } else {
            elements = document.getElementsByTagName(t);
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            var node = elements.item(i);
            var vis = elements.item(i).style;
            for (var j = 0; j < node.attributes.length; j++) {
                if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeName == 'class') {
                    if (node.attributes.item(j).nodeValue == 'rgRow grid_average') {


                        if (browserCheck > 0) {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'block';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'block') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'block'; }
                            }

                        }

                        else {

                            if (vis.display == undefined) {
                                vis.dispaly = 'table-row';
                            }
                            else {
                                if (vis.display == 'table-row') { vis.display = 'none'; } else { vis.display = 'table-row'; }
                            }

                        }

                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // Create the tooltips only on document load
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // Make sure to only match links to wikipedia with a rel tag
        $('a[tipgloss]').each(function () {
            // We make use of the .each() loop to gain access to each element via the "this" keyword...
            $(this).qtip(
		{
		    content: {
		        // Set the text to an image HTML string with the correct src URL to the loading image you want to use
		        text: " ",
		        ajax: {
		            url: $(this).attr('tipgloss') // Use the rel attribute of each element for the url to load
		        }
		    },
		    position: {
		        viewport: $(window),
		        at: "top center",
		        my: "bottom center",
		        effect: false
		    },
		    show: {
		        event: "click mouseenter",
		        solo: true // Only show one tooltip at a time
		    },
		    hide: {
		        event: "click mouseleave",
		        delay: 1000,
		        fixed: true
		    },
		    style: {
		        classes: "ui-tooltip-light"
		    }
		})

            // Make sure it doesn't follow the link when we click it
        });
    });
